---
layout: "post"
title: "Simple Typed Lambda Calculus In Agda"
date: "2018-08-17"
categories: type-theory home
toc: true
agda: true
latex: true
---

We present a formalisation of the syntax in Agda for the *Simple Typed Lambda
Calculus (STLC)* with some of its properties and the description of the
type-checking for this type system. We refactor the implementation by
[@gergoerdi](https://github.com/gergoerdi/stlc-agda/) for this calculus,
in particular the [Scopecheck](https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk/blob/master/src/Scopecheck.agda)
and [Typecheck](https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk/blob/master/src/Typecheck.agda) module.

The following source code was tested with:

- Agda v2.5.4
- Agda Standard Library v0.16

The original content was firstly exposed in the seminar of logic at Universidad EAFIT.

  - [Slides](https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk/raw/master/slides/slides.pdf).
  - Repository: [https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk](https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk).

{: .foldable }

### Bound

Lambda terms using De Bruijn indexes.

Syntax using indexes.

      <a id="3194" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3196" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3114" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="3198" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2748" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="3200" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1513" class="InductiveConstructor">lam</a> <a id="3204" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3205" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3103" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="3207" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1433" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∶</a> <a id="3209" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3105" class="Bound">A</a><a id="3210" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3212" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3107" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="3214" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2748" class="Datatype Operator">⇝</a> <a id="3216" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2452" class="InductiveConstructor">lam</a> <a id="3220" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3105" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3222" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3109" class="Bound">t&#39;</a>

      <a id="3283" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3285" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3263" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="3287" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2748" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="3289" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3247" class="Bound">t₁</a> <a id="3292" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2748" class="Datatype Operator">⇝</a> <a id="3294" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3250" class="Bound">t₁&#39;</a>

### Scopecheck

Check representation of λ-terms using de Bruijn indexes.
Get a λ-term using de Bruijn indexes by given a λ-term with names.

{: .foldable }
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="4296" class="Comment">-- ∃-syntax and ∄-syntax</a>

    <a id="5918" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5920" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5921" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5921" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="5923" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5925" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2622" class="Function">Binder</a> <a id="5932" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5911" class="Bound">n</a><a id="5933" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5935" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5937" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5938" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5938" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="5940" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5942" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1343" class="Function">Name</a><a id="5946" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="5952" class="Comment">------------------------------</a>
    <a id="5987" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5989" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#534" class="Datatype">Dec</a> <a id="5993" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5994" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#4439" class="Function">∃[</a> <a id="5997" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5997" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="5999" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#4439" class="Function">]</a> <a id="6001" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6002" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5921" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="6004" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2748" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="6006" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1489" class="InductiveConstructor">var</a> <a id="6010" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5938" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6012" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2748" class="Datatype Operator">⇝</a> <a id="6014" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5997" class="Bound">t</a><a id="6015" class="Symbol">))</a>

              <a id="6709" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="6714" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5297" class="Function">name-dec</a> <a id="6723" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6683" class="Bound">Γ,y⊢varx⇝t</a>
            <a id="6746" class="Symbol">...</a>  <a id="6751" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="6753" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#470" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="6758" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6758" class="Bound">x≡y</a>                    <a id="6781" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6783" class="Bound">x≢y</a> <a id="6787" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6758" class="Bound">x≡y</a>
            <a id="6803" class="Symbol">...</a>  <a id="6808" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="6810" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#495" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="6815" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6815" class="Bound">p</a><a id="6816" class="Symbol">@(</a><a id="6818" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6818" class="Bound">t′</a> <a id="6821" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">-by-</a> <a id="6826" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6826" class="Bound">Γ⊢varx⇝t′</a><a id="6835" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6837" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6839" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6567" class="Bound">∄t⟨Γ⊢varx⇝t⟩</a> <a id="6852" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6815" class="Bound">p</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We want to determine if given a variable context and a term,
it is possible to find its encoding using De Bruijn indexes.
If so, we got its respective construction for that lambda term.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="Scopecheck.check"></a><a id="7068" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7068" class="Function">check</a>
    <a id="7078" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7080" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="7082" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7083" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7083" class="Bound">n</a><a id="7084" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="7090" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7092" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7093" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7093" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="7095" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7097" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2622" class="Function">Binder</a> <a id="7104" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7083" class="Bound">n</a><a id="7105" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="7111" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7113" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7114" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7114" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="7116" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7118" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1468" class="Datatype">S.Expr</a><a id="7124" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="7130" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7132" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#534" class="Datatype">Dec</a> <a id="7136" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7137" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#4439" class="Function">∃[</a> <a id="7140" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7140" class="Bound">t′</a> <a id="7143" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#4439" class="Function">]</a> <a id="7145" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7146" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7093" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="7148" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2748" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="7150" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7114" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="7152" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2748" class="Datatype Operator">⇝</a> <a id="7154" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7140" class="Bound">t′</a><a id="7156" class="Symbol">))</a>

  <a id="7162" class="Comment">-- By induction on the term syntax.</a>

  <a id="8688" class="Comment">-- Go from a representation that uses Names to one that uses de Bruijn indices</a>
  <a id="Scopecheck.scope"></a><a id="8769" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8769" class="Function">scope</a> <a id="8775" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8777" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8778" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8778" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="8780" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8782" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1468" class="Datatype">S.Expr</a><a id="8788" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8790" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8792" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8793" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8793" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="8795" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8797" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Decidable.html#897" class="Function">True</a> <a id="8802" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8803" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7068" class="Function">check</a> <a id="8809" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Vec.html#712" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a> <a id="8812" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8778" class="Bound">t</a><a id="8813" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="8816" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8818" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2397" class="Datatype">Expr</a> <a id="8823" class="Number">0</a>
  <a id="8827" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8769" class="Function">scope</a> <a id="8833" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8833" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="8835" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8836" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8836" class="Bound">p</a><a id="8837" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8839" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8841" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#155" class="Field">proj₁</a> <a id="8847" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8848" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Decidable.html#1055" class="Function">toWitness</a> <a id="8858" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8836" class="Bound">p</a><a id="8859" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

    <a id="10554" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#10490" class="Function">K</a> <a id="10556" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10558" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9959" class="InductiveConstructor">tLam</a> <a id="10563" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10564" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9959" class="InductiveConstructor">tLam</a> <a id="10569" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9893" class="InductiveConstructor">tVar</a><a id="10573" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="10580" class="Keyword">postulate</a>
      <a id="Typing.A"></a><a id="10596" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#10596" class="Postulate">A</a> <a id="10598" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10600" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9482" class="Datatype">Type</a>
      <a id="Typing.B"></a><a id="10611" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#10611" class="Postulate">B</a> <a id="10613" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10615" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9482" class="Datatype">Type</a>
      <a id="Typing.C"></a><a id="10626" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#10626" class="Postulate">C</a> <a id="10628" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10630" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9482" class="Datatype">Type</a>

    <a id="10640" class="Comment">-- S : [] ⊢ lam (A ↣ (B ↣ C))</a>
    <a id="10674" class="Comment">--              (lam (A ↣ B)</a>
    <a id="10707" class="Comment">--                   (lam A</a>
    <a id="10739" class="Comment">--                     ((var (# 2)) ∙ (var (# 0))) ∙ ((var (# 1)) ∙ (var (# 0))) ))</a>
    <a id="10827" class="Comment">--        ∶ (A ↣ (B ↣ C)) ↣ (A ↣ B) ↣ A ↣ C</a>
    <a id="10875" class="Comment">-- S = tLam (tLam ((tLam ({! tVar  !} ∙ {!   !})) ∙ ({! tVar  !} ∙ {!   !}))) --  tLam (tLam (tLam ((tVar ∙ tVar) ∙ (tVar ∙ tVar))))</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

### References
